property\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.client.OpenLineageClient.config\">\n<em class=\"property\"><span class=\"pre\">property</span><span class=\"w\"> </span></em><span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">config</span></span><em class=\"property\"><span class=\"p\"><span class=\"pre\">:</span></span><span class=\"w\"> </span><a class=\"reference internal\" href=\"#openlineage.client.client.OpenLineageConfig\" title=\"openlineage.client.client.OpenLineageConfig\"><span class=\"pre\">OpenLineageConfig</span></a></em></dt>\n<dd><p>Retrieves the OpenLineage configuration.</p>\n<p>This property method returns the content of the OpenLineage YAML config file.\nThe configuration is determined by merging sources in the following order of precedence:\n1. User-defined configuration passed to the client constructor.\n2. YAML config file located in one of the following paths:\n- Path specified by the <cite>OPENLINEAGE_CONFIG</cite> environment variable.\n- Current working directory.\n- <cite>$HOME/.openlineage</cite>.\n3. Environment variables with the <cite>OPENLINEAGE__</cite> prefix.\nIf the configuration is not already loaded, it will be constructed by merging the above sources.\nIn case of a TypeError during the parsing of the configuration, a ValueError will be raised indicating\nthat the structure of the config does not match the expected format.</p>\n</dd></dl>\n<dl class=\"py method\">\n<dt class=\"sig merges two dictionaries.</p>\n<p>This function merges two dictionaries while handling nested dictionaries.\nFor keys that exist in both dictionaries, the values from dict2 take precedence.\nIf a key exists in both dictionaries and the values are dictionaries themselves,\nthey are merged recursively.\nThis function merges only dictionaries. If key is of different type, e.g. list\nit does not work properly.</p>\n<dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd id=\"module-openlineage.client.uuid\">\n<span id=\"openlineage-client-uuid-module\"></span><h2>openlineage.client.uuid module</h2>\n<dl class=\"py function\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.uuid.generate_new_uuid\">\n<span class=\"sig-prename descclassname\"><span class=\"pre\">openlineage.client.uuid.</span></span><span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">generate_new_uuid</span></span><span class=\"sig-paren\">(</span><em class=\"sig-param\"><span class=\"n\"><span class=\"pre\">instant</span></span><span class=\"o\"><span class=\"pre\">=</span></span><span class=\"default_value\"><span class=\"pre\">None</span></span></em><span class=\"sig-paren\">)</span></dt>\n<dd><p>Generate new UUID for an instant of time. Each function call returns a new UUID value.</p>\n<p>UUID version is an implementation detail, and <strong>should not</strong> be relied on.\nFor now it is [UUIDv7](<a class=\"reference external\" href=\"https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/\">https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/</a>), so for increasing instant values,\nreturned UUID is always greater than previous one.</p>\n<p>Using uuid6 lib implementation (MIT License), with few changes:\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L128-L147\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a>\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L46-L51\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a></p>\n<p>Added in v1.15.0</p>\n<dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><p><strong>instant</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">datetime | None</span>) \u2013 instant of time used to generate UUID. If not provided, current time is used.</p>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-even\">Return type<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-even\"><p><span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">UUID</span></p>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Returns<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><p>UUID</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</dd></dl>\n<dl class=\"py function\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.uuid.generate_static_uuid\">\n<span class=\"sig-prename descclassname\"><span class=\"pre\">openlineage.client.uuid.</span></span><span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">generate_static_uuid</span></span><span class=\"sig-paren\">(</span><em class=\"sig-param\"><span class=\"n\"><span class=\"pre\">instant</span></span></em>, <em class=\"sig-param\"><span class=\"n\"><span class=\"pre\">data</span></span></em><span class=\"sig-paren\">)</span></dt>\n<dd><p>Generate UUID for instant of time and input data.\nCalling function with same arguments always produces the same result.</p>\n<p>UUID version is an implementation detail, and <a href=\"#id1\"><span class=\"problematic\" id=\"id2\">**</span></a>should not* be relied on.\nFor now it is [UUIDv7](<a class=\"reference external\" href=\"https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/\">https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/</a>), so for increasing instant values,\nreturned UUID is always greater than previous one. The only difference from RFC 9562 is that\nleast significant bytes are not random, but instead a SHA-1 hash of input data.</p>\n<p>Using uuid6 lib implementation (MIT License), with few changes:\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L128-L147\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a>\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L46-L51\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a></p>\n<p>Added in v1.15.0</p>\n<dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><p><strong>instant</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\"><code class=\"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate\"><span class=\"pre\">datetime</span></code></span>) \u2013 instant of time used to generate UUID. If not provided, current time is used.</p></li>\n<li><p><strong>data</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\"><code class=\"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate\"><span class=\"pre\">bytes</span></code></span>) \u2013 input data to generate random part from.</p></li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-even\">Return type<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-even\"><p><span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\"><code class=\"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate\"><span class=\"pre\">UUID</span></code></span></p>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Returns<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><p>UUID</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</dd></dl>\n</section>\n<section id=\"openlineage.client.transport.composite.CompositeConfig.transports\">\n<span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">transports</span></span></dt>\n<dd><p>A list or dict of dictionaries, where each dictionary represents the configuration\nfor a child transport. Each dictionary should contain the necessary parameters\nto initialize a specific transport instance. If dict of dictionaries is passed,\nkeys of the dict will be treated as transport names.</p>\n</dd></dl>\n<dl class=\"py attribute\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.transport.composite.CompositeConfig.continue_on_failure\">\n<span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">continue_on_failure</span></span></dt>\n<dd><p>If set to True, the CompositeTransport will attempt to emit the event using\nall configured transports, regardless of whether any previous transport\nin the list failed to emit the event. If none of the transports successfully emit\nthe event, an error will still be raised at the end to indicate that no events were emitted.\nIf set to False, an error in transport will halt the emission process for subsequent transports.</p>\n</dd></dl>\n<dl class=\"py attribute\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.transport.composite.CompositeConfig.continue_on_success\">\n<span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">continue_on_success</span></span></dt>\n<dd><p>If True, the CompositeTransport will continue emitting events to all transports\neven after a successful delivery. If False, it will stop emitting to other\ntransports as soon as the first successful delivery occurs.</p>\n</dd></dl>\n<dl class=\"py attribute\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.transport.composite.CompositeConfig.sort_transports\">\n<span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">sort_transports</span></span></dt>\n<dd><p>If True, transports will be sorted before emission by <cite>priority</cite> field.\nIf False, order of transports will not be changed.</p>\n</dd></dl>\n<dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>Continue behavior summary:</dt><dd><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>continue_on_failure=True, continue_on_success=True:</dt><dd><p>Always emits to all transports, regardless of successes or failures. Events are delivered\neverywhere, with no early termination.</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</li>\n<li><dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>continue_on_failure=True, continue_on_success=False:</dt><dd><p>Stops on the first successful emission. Failures are ignored and transports continue to be\ntried until a success is found.</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</li>\n<li><dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>continue_on_failure=False, continue_on_success=False:</dt><dd><p>Stops on the first success or the first failure, whichever occurs first.</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</li>\n<li><dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>continue_on_failure=False, continue_on_success=True:</dt><dd><p>Stops immediately on the first failure (fail-fast). However, if no failures occur, events will be\nemitted to all transports, effectively behaving like a \u201cfail-fast all\u201d strategy. This behavior\nmay not align with typical expectations when an early stop after a success is desired; review\ncarefully to ensure it matches the intended delivery semantics.</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n<dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><p><strong>transports</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">list[dict[str, Any]] | dict[str, dict[str, Any]]</span>)</p></li>\n<li><p><strong>continue_on_failure</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">bool</span>)</p></li>\n<li><p><strong>continue_on_success</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">bool</span>)</p></li>\n<li><p><strong>sort_transports</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">bool</span>)</p></li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n<dl for OpenLineage events.</p>\n<p>Writes events to local or remote files. Supports automatic protocol detection\nfor remote filesystems via fsspec (s3://, gs://, az://, etc.).</p>\n<p>Three filesystem configuration approaches:\n1. Auto-detection: Specify only log_file_path with protocol URL\n2. Explicit filesystem: Use \u2018filesystem\u2019 parameter with class/factory/instance\n3. Storage options: Use \u2018storage_options\u2019 for credentials and configuration</p>\n<dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd complete until the timeout is reached.</p>\n<dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>Params:</dt><dd><p>timeout: Timeout in seconds. id=\"openlineage-client-transport-transport-module\"></span><h2>openlineage.client.transport.transport module</h2>\n<p>Transport interface for OpenLineage events.</p>\n<p>To implement a custom Transport, implement both Config and Transport classes.</p>\n<dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>Transport implementation requirements:</dt><dd><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><p>Specify class variable <cite>config_class</cite> that points to the Config class that Transport requires</p></li>\n<li><p>Implement <cite>__init__</cite> that accepts the specified Config class instance</p></li>\n<li><p>Implement <cite>emit</cite> method that accepts OpenLineage events</p></li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n<dt>Config implementation requirements:</dt><dd><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><p>Implement <cite>from_dict</cite> classmethod to create config from dictionary parameters</p></li>\n<li><p>The config class can have complex attributes, but must be able to instantiate them in <cite>from_dict</cite></p></li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n<dt>Transport instantiation:</dt><dd><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><p>TransportFactory instantiates custom transports by looking at the <cite>type</cite> field in the config</p></li>\n<li><p>The factory uses this type to determine which transport class to instantiate</p></li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n<dl class=\"py class\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.transport.transport.Config\">\n<em class=\"property\"><span class=\"pre\">class</span><span class=\"w\"> </span></em><span class=\"sig-prename
